-- ======================================================================
-- SHUTTLE_UP — MỘT FILE, CHẠY MỘT LẦN (single source of truth)
-- ======================================================================
-- Chỉ cần script này: không chạy thêm file migration rời cho venues (includes / rules /
-- amenities), payment VietQR, refund_requests, v.v. — tất cả đã gộp (CREATE + khối ALTER
-- có điều kiện ở cuối).
--
-- Schema + dữ liệu mẫu: CHỈ sửa file này — không dùng thêm file .sql rời trong repo.
-- Khi cần DB sạch đồng bộ code: chạy lại TOÀN BỘ script từ dòng CREATE DATABASE trở xuống.
--
-- Cách chạy:
--   • MySQL Workbench: kết nối server → mở file này → Ctrl+A → Execute toàn bộ.
--   • CLI: mysql -u ... -p < Database.txt   (hoặc: SOURCE đường_dẫn/Database.txt)
--
-- Lưu ý:
--   • Script có DROP TABLE + CREATE + INSERT mẫu → phù hợp reset môi trường dev / DB mới.
--   • Phần ALTER cuối file kiểm tra information_schema: cột đã có thì bỏ qua (an toàn
--     nếu bạn chỉ paste chạy phần migration trên DB cũ cần giữ dữ liệu — nguồn chuẩn vẫn là file này).
--   • Backend: ConnectionStrings:DefaultConnection → database=shuttle_up
--     (ShuttleUp.Backend/appsettings.json); có thể ghi đè bằng biến môi trường.
--   • Workbench: luôn USE shuttle_up; hoặc chọn schema shuttle_up ở panel trái; bôi đen một đoạn thì DATABASE() có thể lệch.
--
-- Nếu API báo "Unknown column ...":
--   1) Xác nhận backend đang trỏ đúng server/DB (mặc định shuttle_up).
--   2) Chạy lại full Database.txt; tránh chỉ chạy nửa file nếu chưa rà soát thứ tự DROP/CREATE.
--   Ví dụ matching (parent_comment_id, v.v.): migration nằm trong file này.
--
-- Trang /featured trống: phải có bảng featured_posts + INSERT mẫu (phần FEATURED POSTS MẪU). Nếu chạy lại script mà thiếu DROP featured_posts
-- thì CREATE TABLE featured_posts có thể lỗi "already exists" và phần sau không chạy — đã có DROP featured_posts trong khối VENUE.
-- ======================================================================
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS shuttle_up;
USE shuttle_up;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0;

-- FILE MAPPINGS
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS report_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS court_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venue_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venue_review_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS chat_message_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS refund_request_files;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS files;

-- ADMIN
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS violation_report_logs;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS violation_reports;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS manager_profiles;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS manager_profile_requests;

-- REVIEWS
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS favorite_venues;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venue_reviews;

-- CHAT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS chat_room_members;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS chat_messages;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS chat_rooms;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS matching_post_comments;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS matching_members;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS matching_join_requests;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS matching_post_items;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS matching_posts;

-- PAYMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS refund_transactions;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS refund_requests;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS payments;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS user_notifications;

-- BOOKING
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS court_blocks;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS court_open_hours;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS booking_items;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bookings;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS booking_series;

-- VENUE
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venue_coupons;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS featured_posts;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS court_prices;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venue_open_hours;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS courts;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS venues;

-- USERS (social — trước user_roles/users)
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS friend_requests;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS friendships;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS user_blocks;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS user_privacy_settings;

-- USERS
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS user_roles;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS roles;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users;

-- ======================================================================
-- USERS
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE users (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    phone_number VARCHAR(20),
    about TEXT,
    address VARCHAR(500),
    district VARCHAR(100),
    province VARCHAR(100),
    gender VARCHAR(20),
    date_of_birth DATE,
    skill_level VARCHAR(50) NULL,
    play_purpose VARCHAR(100) NULL,
    play_frequency VARCHAR(50) NULL,
    is_personalized BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    blocked_at DATETIME,
    blocked_reason TEXT,
    ban_type VARCHAR(10) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
    soft_ban_expires_at DATETIME NULL DEFAULT NULL,
    blocked_by CHAR(36),
    avatar_file_id CHAR(36),
    auth_provider VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'LOCAL' COMMENT 'LOCAL | GOOGLE',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE roles (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL
);

INSERT INTO roles VALUES
('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001','ADMIN'),
('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000002','PLAYER'),
('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003','MANAGER');

CREATE TABLE user_roles (
    user_id CHAR(36),
    role_id CHAR(36),
    PRIMARY KEY(user_id,role_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES roles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- ======================================================================
-- USER SOCIAL (kết bạn, chặn, quyền riêng tư tìm kiếm)
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE user_privacy_settings (
    user_id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    allow_find_by_email TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    allow_find_by_phone TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE user_blocks (
    blocker_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    blocked_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    PRIMARY KEY (blocker_id, blocked_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (blocker_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (blocked_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    INDEX idx_user_blocks_blocked (blocked_id)
);

CREATE TABLE friendships (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_low_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    user_high_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY uk_friend_pair (user_low_id, user_high_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_low_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_high_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE friend_requests (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    from_user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    to_user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    responded_at DATETIME NULL,
    INDEX idx_friend_req_to_status (to_user_id, status),
    INDEX idx_friend_req_from_status (from_user_id, status),
    FOREIGN KEY (from_user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (to_user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE manager_profiles (
    user_id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    tax_code VARCHAR(50),
    address TEXT,
    cccd_front_file_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    cccd_back_file_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_1 CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_2 CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_3 CHAR(36) NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    admin_user_id CHAR(36),
    decision_at DATETIME,
    decision_note TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- MANAGER PROFILE REQUESTS (LỊCH SỬ DUYỆT)
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE manager_profile_requests (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    request_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- DANG_KY | CAP_NHAT
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING' NOT NULL,
    requested_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    tax_code VARCHAR(50),
    address TEXT,
    cccd_front_file_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    cccd_back_file_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_1 CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_2 CHAR(36) NULL,
    business_license_file_id_3 CHAR(36) NULL,
    admin_user_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    decision_at DATETIME NULL,
    decision_note TEXT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    INDEX idx_manager_profile_requests_user_status_requested (user_id, status, requested_at)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- VENUES
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE venues (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    owner_user_id CHAR(36),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    address TEXT NOT NULL,
    lat DECIMAL(10,8),
    lng DECIMAL(11,8),
    description TEXT,
    weekly_discount_percent DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    monthly_discount_percent DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    payment_bank_name VARCHAR(100) NULL COMMENT 'Display name e.g. Vietcombank',
    payment_bank_bin VARCHAR(20) NULL COMMENT '6-digit VietQR bank ID',
    payment_account_number VARCHAR(50) NULL,
    payment_account_holder VARCHAR(255) NULL,
    payment_transfer_note_template VARCHAR(500) NULL DEFAULT '[SĐT] - [Tên sân] - [Ngày]',
    payment_note VARCHAR(1000) NULL COMMENT 'Ghi chú hướng dẫn thanh toán cho người chơi',
    cancel_allowed TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    cancel_before_minutes INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 120,
    slot_duration INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 60,
    refund_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'NONE' COMMENT 'NONE|PERCENT|FULL',
    refund_percent DECIMAL(5,2) NULL,
    thumbnail_file_id CHAR(36),
    contact_name VARCHAR(255),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(50),
    includes JSON NULL COMMENT 'Mảng chuỗi — những gì khách được sử dụng khi thuê sân',
    rules JSON NULL COMMENT 'Mảng chuỗi — các quy định tại cơ sở',
    amenities JSON NULL COMMENT 'Mảng key chuỗi — tiện ích có tại cơ sở (parking, wifi, ...)',
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (owner_user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (thumbnail_file_id) REFERENCES files(id)
);

CREATE TABLE courts (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    name VARCHAR(100),
    group_name VARCHAR(100) NULL,
    surface VARCHAR(50),
    max_guest INT,
    description TEXT,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'ACTIVE',
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE venue_open_hours (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    day_of_week INT,
    open_time TIME,
    close_time TIME,
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- Bài đăng trang Nổi bật (Admin + Manager quảng cáo). Thứ tự công khai: created_at giảm dần.
CREATE TABLE featured_posts (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    excerpt VARCHAR(500) NULL,
    body TEXT NULL,
    cover_image_url VARCHAR(2048) NULL,
    link_url VARCHAR(2048) NULL,
    is_published TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    display_from DATETIME NULL COMMENT 'NULL = không giới hạn đầu',
    display_until DATETIME NULL COMMENT 'NULL = không giới hạn cuối',
    author_user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    author_role VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'ADMIN | MANAGER',
    venue_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    created_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (author_user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    INDEX idx_featured_posts_published_dates (is_published, display_from, display_until),
    INDEX idx_featured_posts_author (author_user_id)
);
-- Dữ liệu mẫu featured_posts: xem phần FEATURED POSTS MẪU (sau VENUES MẪU)

CREATE TABLE court_prices (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    court_id CHAR(36),
    start_time TIME,
    end_time TIME,
    price DECIMAL(15,2),
    is_weekend BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    FOREIGN KEY (court_id) REFERENCES courts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE court_open_hours (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    court_id CHAR(36),
    day_of_week INT,
    open_time TIME NULL,
    close_time TIME NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (court_id) REFERENCES courts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    UNIQUE KEY uq_court_open_hours (court_id, day_of_week)
);

CREATE TABLE venue_coupons (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    venue_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    discount_type VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'PERCENT' COMMENT 'PERCENT|FIXED_AMOUNT',
    discount_value DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    min_booking_value DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    max_discount_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NULL,
    start_date DATETIME NOT NULL,
    end_date DATETIME NOT NULL,
    usage_limit INT NULL,
    used_count INT DEFAULT 0,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    one_use_per_user BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE COMMENT 'TRUE: mỗi user chỉ dùng mã 1 lần (đơn không huỷ)',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    UNIQUE KEY uq_venue_coupon (venue_id, code)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- BOOKING
-- ======================================================================
-- booking_series.recurrence_rule_json (ứng dụng quy ước, không enforce ở DB):
--   WEEKLY: { "type":"WEEKLY", "daysOfWeek":[...], "sessionStart","sessionEnd", "courtId" }
--   FLEXIBLE: { "type":"FLEXIBLE", "itemCount": N } — range_start_date/range_end_date = min/max ngày từ booking_items

CREATE TABLE booking_series (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    venue_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    recurrence_rule_json TEXT NOT NULL,
    range_start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    range_end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id),
    INDEX booking_series_user_id (user_id),
    INDEX booking_series_venue_id (venue_id)
);

CREATE TABLE bookings (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id CHAR(36),
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    series_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    coupon_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    hold_expires_at DATETIME NULL COMMENT 'UTC deadline for HOLDING status; NULL when not holding',
    total_amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    discount_amount DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    final_amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    contact_name VARCHAR(255) NULL,
    contact_phone VARCHAR(50) NULL,
    guest_note TEXT NULL,
    manager_status_note VARCHAR(1000) NULL,
    cancellation_policy_snapshot_json TEXT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (series_id) REFERENCES booking_series(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (coupon_id) REFERENCES venue_coupons(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    INDEX series_id (series_id)
);

CREATE TABLE user_notifications (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'BOOKING',
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    body TEXT NULL,
    metadata_json TEXT NULL,
    is_read TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    is_deleted TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_user_notifications_user_created (user_id, created_at),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE booking_items (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id CHAR(36),
    court_id CHAR(36),
    start_time DATETIME,
    end_time DATETIME,
    final_price DECIMAL(15,2),
    status VARCHAR(50),
    is_upcoming_reminder_sent TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT 'Cờ đánh dấu đã gửi nhắc nhở sắp đến giờ',
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (court_id) REFERENCES courts(id),
    INDEX idx_bi_reminder (start_time, is_upcoming_reminder_sent)
);

CREATE TABLE court_blocks (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    court_id CHAR(36),
    start_time DATETIME,
    end_time DATETIME,
    created_by CHAR(36),
    reason_code VARCHAR(30) NULL COMMENT 'MAINTENANCE|WEATHER|OTHER',
    reason_detail VARCHAR(500) NULL COMMENT 'Hiển thị cho người chơi',
    internal_note VARCHAR(500) NULL COMMENT 'Ghi chú nội bộ chủ sân',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (court_id) REFERENCES courts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (created_by) REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- PAYMENTS
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE payments (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id CHAR(36),
    method VARCHAR(50),
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    gateway_reference VARCHAR(255),
    confirmed_by CHAR(36),
    confirmed_at DATETIME,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (confirmed_by) REFERENCES users(id)
);

CREATE TABLE refund_requests (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id CHAR(36),
    user_id CHAR(36),
    reason_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PLAYER_CANCEL' COMMENT 'PLAYER_CANCEL|MANAGER_CANCEL|ADMIN',
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING' COMMENT 'PENDING_RECONCILIATION|PENDING_REFUND|COMPLETED|REJECTED',
    requested_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NULL COMMENT 'Số tiền hoàn dự kiến theo snapshot',
    paid_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NULL COMMENT 'Số tiền đã thu (snapshot lúc tạo yêu cầu)',
    refund_bank_name VARCHAR(100) NULL COMMENT 'NH nhận hoàn (Player nhập)',
    refund_account_number VARCHAR(50) NULL,
    refund_account_holder VARCHAR(255) NULL,
    refund_qr_image_url VARCHAR(2048) NULL COMMENT 'Ảnh mã QR nhận hoàn tiền (Cloudinary URL)',
    player_note TEXT NULL,
    rejection_reason TEXT NULL,
    manager_note TEXT NULL,
    manager_evidence_file_id CHAR(36) NULL COMMENT 'Ảnh bill CK hoàn từ Manager',
    player_received_file_id CHAR(36) NULL COMMENT 'Ảnh xác nhận nhận tiền từ Player (tùy chọn)',
    requested_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    processed_by CHAR(36),
    processed_at DATETIME,
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (processed_by) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (manager_evidence_file_id) REFERENCES files(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (player_received_file_id) REFERENCES files(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    INDEX idx_refund_requests_status (status),
    INDEX idx_refund_requests_booking (booking_id)
);

CREATE TABLE refund_transactions (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    refund_request_id CHAR(36),
    payment_id CHAR(36),
    amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    method VARCHAR(50),
    status VARCHAR(50),
    gateway_reference VARCHAR(255),
    processed_by CHAR(36),
    processed_at DATETIME,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (refund_request_id) REFERENCES refund_requests(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (payment_id) REFERENCES payments(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (processed_by) REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- MATCHING
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE matching_posts (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    creator_user_id CHAR(36),
    booking_id CHAR(36),
    title VARCHAR(255),
    play_date DATE,
    play_start_time TIME,
    play_end_time TIME,
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    court_name VARCHAR(100),
    price_per_slot DECIMAL(15,2),
    required_players INT,
    skill_level VARCHAR(50),
    gender_pref VARCHAR(50),
    expense_sharing VARCHAR(100),
    play_purpose VARCHAR(100),
    notes TEXT,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'OPEN',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (creator_user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id),
    INDEX idx_matching_posts_status_date (status, play_date),
    INDEX idx_matching_posts_creator (creator_user_id)
);

CREATE TABLE matching_post_items (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    booking_item_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (post_id) REFERENCES matching_posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_item_id) REFERENCES booking_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    UNIQUE KEY uq_post_booking_item (post_id, booking_item_id)
);

CREATE TABLE matching_join_requests (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id CHAR(36),
    user_id CHAR(36),
    message TEXT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    reject_reason TEXT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (post_id) REFERENCES matching_posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    INDEX idx_matching_join_post_status (post_id, status)
);

CREATE TABLE matching_members (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id CHAR(36),
    user_id CHAR(36),
    joined_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (post_id) REFERENCES matching_posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    UNIQUE KEY uq_matching_member (post_id, user_id)
);

CREATE TABLE matching_post_comments (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    parent_comment_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME NULL,
    is_deleted TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    deleted_at DATETIME NULL,
    deleted_by_user_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    attachment_file_id CHAR(36) NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (post_id) REFERENCES matching_posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    CONSTRAINT matching_post_comments_parent_fk FOREIGN KEY (parent_comment_id) REFERENCES matching_post_comments(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    CONSTRAINT matching_post_comments_deleted_by_fk FOREIGN KEY (deleted_by_user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    CONSTRAINT matching_post_comments_attachment_fk FOREIGN KEY (attachment_file_id) REFERENCES files(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    INDEX idx_matching_comments_post (post_id, created_at),
    INDEX idx_matching_comments_post_active (post_id, is_deleted, created_at)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- CHAT
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE chat_rooms (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255),
    created_by CHAR(36),
    post_id CHAR(36) UNIQUE,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (created_by) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (post_id) REFERENCES matching_posts(id) ON DELETE SET NULL
);

CREATE TABLE chat_room_members (
    room_id CHAR(36),
    user_id CHAR(36),
    joined_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    PRIMARY KEY(room_id,user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (room_id) REFERENCES chat_rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE chat_messages (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    chat_room_id CHAR(36),
    sender_user_id CHAR(36),
    message_text TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (chat_room_id) REFERENCES chat_rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (sender_user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- REVIEWS
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE venue_reviews (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    user_id CHAR(36),
    booking_id CHAR(36),
    stars INT CHECK (stars BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
    comment TEXT,
    owner_reply TEXT NULL COMMENT 'Phản hồi của chủ sân (manager)',
    owner_reply_at DATETIME NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id)
);

CREATE TABLE favorite_venues (
    user_id CHAR(36),
    venue_id CHAR(36),
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    PRIMARY KEY(user_id,venue_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- ======================================================================
-- ADMIN
-- ======================================================================


-- target_type: 'USER' | 'VENUE' | 'MATCHING_POST' | 'BOOKING' (dispute)
-- status: 'PENDING' | 'REVIEWING' | 'RESOLVED' | 'REJECTED'
-- admin_action: 'WARN_USER' | 'LOCK_USER' | 'WARN_VENUE' | 'LOCK_VENUE' | 'REMOVE_POST' | 'REFUND' | 'NO_ACTION'
CREATE TABLE violation_reports (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    reporter_user_id CHAR(36),
    target_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    target_id CHAR(36),
    reason VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    -- PENDING | REVIEWING | REFUND_PENDING | RESOLVED | REJECTED (REFUND_PENDING = admin đã yêu cầu hoàn tiền, chờ chủ sân thực hiện)
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'PENDING',
    admin_user_id CHAR(36),
    admin_note TEXT,
    admin_action VARCHAR(50),
    decision_at DATETIME,
    refund_deadline_at DATETIME NULL COMMENT 'Hạn SLA hoàn tiền khi status=REFUND_PENDING',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_violation_reports_target (target_type, target_id),
    INDEX idx_violation_reports_status_created (status, created_at),
    INDEX idx_violation_reports_created (created_at),
    INDEX idx_violation_reports_refund_sla (status, refund_deadline_at),
    FOREIGN KEY (reporter_user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

CREATE TABLE violation_report_logs (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    report_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    admin_user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    admin_action VARCHAR(50),
    admin_note TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (report_id) REFERENCES violation_reports(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ======================================================================
-- FILE STORAGE
-- ======================================================================

CREATE TABLE files (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    file_url VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    file_name VARCHAR(255),
    mime_type VARCHAR(50),
    file_size INT,
    uploaded_by_user_id CHAR(36),
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (uploaded_by_user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

    review_id CHAR(36),

    venue_id CHAR(36),

-- Migration: DB đã tồn tại (không chạy full script từ đầu) — bỏ comment và chạy một lần nếu thiếu cột
-- ======================================================================
-- Bảng booking_series + cột bookings.series_id (đặt lịch dài hạn)
SET @tbl_exists := (
  SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.tables
  WHERE table_schema = DATABASE() AND table_name = 'booking_series'
);
SET @sql := IF(@tbl_exists = 0,
  'CREATE TABLE booking_series (
    id CHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    venue_id CHAR(36) NOT NULL,
    recurrence_rule_json TEXT NOT NULL,
    range_start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    range_end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT ''PENDING'',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id),
    INDEX booking_series_user_id (user_id),
    INDEX booking_series_venue_id (venue_id)
  )',
  'DO 0');
PREPARE stmt FROM @sql; EXECUTE stmt; DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt;

SET @col_exists := (
  SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.columns
  WHERE table_schema = DATABASE() AND table_name = 'bookings' AND column_name = 'series_id'
);
SET @sql := IF(@col_exists = 0,
  'ALTER TABLE bookings ADD COLUMN series_id CHAR(36) NULL, ADD INDEX series_id (series_id), ADD CONSTRAINT bookings_series_fk FOREIGN KEY (series_id) REFERENCES booking_series(id) ON DELETE SET NULL',
  'DO 0');
PREPARE stmt FROM @sql; EXECUTE stmt; DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt;

SELECT 'Users'    AS entity, COUNT(*) AS total FROM users      UNION ALL
SELECT 'Venues',              COUNT(*)          FROM venues     UNION ALL
SELECT 'Courts',              COUNT(*)          FROM courts     UNION ALL
SELECT 'Files',               COUNT(*)          FROM files      UNION ALL
SELECT 'VenueFiles',          COUNT(*)          FROM venue_files UNION ALL
SELECT 'FeaturedPosts',       COUNT(*)          FROM featured_posts UNION ALL
SELECT 'Reviews',             COUNT(*)          FROM venue_reviews;

SET @col_sd := (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_schema = DATABASE() AND table_name = 'venues' AND column_name = 'slot_duration');

PREPARE stmt_sd FROM @sql_sd; EXECUTE stmt_sd; DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt_sd;

SELECT 'Users' AS entity, COUNT(*) AS total FROM users UNION ALL
SELECT 'Venues', COUNT(*) FROM venues UNION ALL
SELECT 'Courts', COUNT(*) FROM courts UNION ALL
SELECT 'Bookings', COUNT(*) FROM bookings UNION ALL
SELECT 'BookingItems', COUNT(*) FROM booking_items UNION ALL
SELECT 'Payments', COUNT(*) FROM payments UNION ALL
SELECT 'Reviews', COUNT(*) FROM venue_reviews UNION ALL
SELECT 'MatchingPosts', COUNT(*) FROM matching_posts UNION ALL
SELECT 'ChatRooms', COUNT(*) FROM chat_rooms UNION ALL
SELECT 'ChatMessages', COUNT(*) FROM chat_messages UNION ALL
SELECT 'FeaturedPosts', COUNT(*) FROM featured_posts UNION ALL
SELECT 'Coupons', COUNT(*) FROM venue_coupons UNION ALL
SELECT 'Favorites', COUNT(*) FROM favorite_venues UNION ALL
SELECT 'ManagerProfiles', COUNT(*) FROM manager_profiles UNION ALL
SELECT 'ViolationReports', COUNT(*) FROM violation_reports;
